 Shocking definitions The report of a task force of the Policy Commission says that relevant and accurate figures do not exist because there is no uniformity in the definitions used for workers
 udhaaharan ke taur par bharat main sangathit (formal) kamgaaron ke liye paribhaasha tay nahin he isliye kai paribhaashaayen istemaal hoti hai
 The most common definition applies to people working in registered enterprises under the Factories Act, 1948, that they are organized workers
 haalanki, eneseso apane survey main inhen formal kii jagah orgenised likhata he
 Under this definition, all workers working in the service sector will be called informal 'or' unorganized workers
 isse alag, shram evam rojgaar mantralay kamgaaron ke vargeekaran ke liye duusari paribhaasha istemaal karata he

 chidambaram) ke vichaar par bharosa dilaanaa chahta hum ki aarthik susti aage jari nahin rahegi

 The Bill will be sent to the Union Law Ministry, Union Ministry of Home Affairs and Ministry of Personnel and Training for detailed interpretation
 iskaa arth yah he ki ise dobaaraa mantrimandal ke paas le jane kii aavashyaktaa nahin he, balki sidhe sansad main pesh kiya jayega

 malaysia kii company teen karod dollar se chah karod dollar tak nivesh kar sakati he

 chatha board sadsy ek bhartiya naagarik hoga or use board ke gaiyr-kaaryakari adhyaksh ke rup main niyukt kiya jayega

 pichley saal sarkaar ne gharelu vimaanan companiyon main videshi vimaanan company ko 49 fisadi nivesh kii anumati di thi

 vidheyak kii vistrut vyakhya ke liye kendriya kanoon mantralay, kendriya grih mantralay or carmik evam prashikshan mantralay main bheja jayega
 This means that it does not need to be taken back to the Cabinet again, but will be introduced directly in Parliament
 vidheyak main kisi bhi seva kii adaayagi main vifal rahane par pratidin 250 rupee se adhiktam 50 hajaar rupee tak ke jurmaana kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he

 Cyclone Ockhi cruising in the Arabian Sea has become more dangerous now
 mausam vibhaag ke mutabik is samay yah dakshin purv arab sagar main he
 According to the swirling winds inside the cyclone, it is now considered to be a very severe cyclone
 isamen 150 se 170 kilometre prati ghante kii raftaar se tej hawaaen chal rahi he or hawa ke jhonkon kii raftaar 180 kilometre prati ghante tak pahunch ja rahi he
 According to the Cyclone Center of the Meteorological Department, now this cyclone is moving away from Lakshadweep
 lakshadweep samooh se tufaan 18 kilometre prati ghante kii raftaar se dur hat rahaa he
 It is expected that the strength of this cyclone will start decreasing from the morning of December 3, but after this the storm will start turning towards Gujarat
 aisa anumaan he ki 3 disambar khatm hote-hote is main hawaaon kii raftaar 135 se 145 kilometre prati ghante kii rah jaaegi
 On 4 December, this cyclone will move towards the Gulf of Khambhat, but as it moves towards Gujarat, its strength will decrease, by the end of 4 December, the speed of strong winds will be 90 to 60 kilometers per hour, but In this situation, the new storm will remain in the category of severe cyclone
 is dauraan uttar maharashtra ke konkan ke ilaakon main samandar main oonchi-oonchi lehren uthne lagegi or isi ke saath samudri kinaaron par 40 se 50 kilometre prati ghante kii raftaar se hawaaon kaa silsilaa shuru ho jayega
 This trend of strong winds will be seen in all areas along the Gulf of Khambhat
 is baat kii ashanka ko dekhte hue mausam vibhaag ne 4 disambar se uttar maharashtra or dakshini gujarat ke sabhi ilaakon main machuaaron ko samandar main naa jane kii salaah di he

" ' bayaan main likhaa gaya he ki vaarta sauhardpurn or rachanaatmak maahaul main yojit kii gai
 It is worth noting that before the United Nations Climate Change Summit in Paris, there was a meeting between Prime Minister Narendra Modi and his Pakistani counterpart Nawaz Sharif
 haalanki, donon netaaon ne adhik samay tak baatcheet nahin kii thi, lekin aamanaa-saamana hone par donon garmjoshi ke saath mili the
 Whereas earlier this year, the nsa-level talks between India and Pakistan were canceled as the two sides could not agree on a meeting agenda
 jaahir taur par donon deshon ke bich baatcheet kaa silsilaa phir se shuru ho gaya he or ummid jataai ja rahi he ki donon mulkon ke rishton main mithaas ghulegi

 ayodhya ram mandir kaa vivaad abhi supreme court main chal rahaa he
 But the land acquired to install the statue of Lord Rama on the banks of the Saryu River in Ayodhya has also come under controversy
 yah bhoomi yogi adityanath sarkaar ne adhigrahit kii thi
 The 64 landowners have approached the Lucknow bench of the Allahabad High Court regarding the manner in which the administration has acquired the land, where their petition has been accepted
 iske liye hai court ne prashasan adhikariyon or jameen maalikon ko apana paksh rakhane ke liye 25 july ko pesh hone ke liye taarikh tay kii he
 The Yogi government of Uttar Pradesh had announced the construction of a statue of Lord Rama, the world's tallest god on the banks of Saryu in Ayodhya, so that every person passing through Ayodhya can see Rama
 iske liye ayodhya jila prashasan ke bhoomi adhigrahan kii prakriya karte hi vivaad khadaa ho gaya he
 The owners of 64 land have raised questions about land acquisition and have reached court with cases
 jameen maalikon kaa kahana he ki ram kii pratimaa lagaae jane par koi aitraaj nahin he, lekin prashasan unhen lagaataar gumraah kar rahaa he
 They allege that proper compensation was not given to the said land
 aise main tinkaa-tinkaa ikattha karke unhone apana ashiana banaaya
 Where to go now unhone kaha ki bhagwaan ram kabhi nahin chahenge ki kisi ko ujaad kar takalif pahunchaai jaae
 The petitioner Awadhesh Singh said, the Yogi government announced the installation of the idol of Lord Ram
 isse ham log khush the
 But it was not known that the idol would be built by destroying us
 lekhpal or prashasan ham logon ko lagaataar gumraah karata rahaa
 That is why we had to go to the court, because these people are not telling about compensation
 balki jabaran jameen jabaran lenaa chaahate hai
 He said, We are not anti-ram, Ram is a devotee
 aisa bhi nahin he ki ham jameen dena nahin chaahate
 But we should be given appropriate compensation

e
 the fuel of the aircraft under the purview of GST

 GST was implemented on July 1 last year
 is dauraanpetrol-dijal,kaccha tel, prakritik gas or vimaan eendhan sareekhe paanch utpaadon ko isse baahar rakhaa gaya tha

 ab jabaki is vyavastha ko lagu hue ek saal puraa ho chukaa he, to prakritik gas or jet ful ko iske daayre main laane par vichaar kiya ja rahaa he

 kyonki maujuuda vakt main jet ful par centre kaa utpaada shulk 14 fisadi he
